Administration of how important things are for democracy

[For question D28, we are including five different versions with the order of the response items rotated by one position each time. The filter variable for this (D28Order) is described below. Each respondent should be randomly assigned to one of the five versions. There are also five different showcards for these items to reflect the different orders. Create random split variable D28Order which will NOT BE SHOWN to respondents. Each experimental group should include approximately 20% of respondents. This variable should be populated at the start of the interview. It is also required to build in CAPI hard checks at D28CheckA/B/C/D/E. At each of these, interviewers must be asked to confirm that the correct showcard is being used before they are allowed to progress to the next question.]

emplrel
Employment relation

INTERVIEWER: If respondent currently in work, F21 to F34a refer to their current job; if not in paid work but had a job in the past, F21 to F34a refer to their last job. INTERVIEWER: If the respondent has more than one job, they should answer about the one which occupies them for the most hours per week. If they have two jobs that are exactly equal, they should answer about the more highly paid of the two.
